### 用户

import pybullet as p
import numpy as np
from scipy.spatial.transform import Rotation as R
import gymnasium as gym
from gymnasium import spaces
from gymnasium.utils import seeding
from typing import Optional
from gymnasium.envs.registration import register
import time

class Observation:
    def __init__(self, pos=None, orn = None, euler=None):
        self.pos = pos
        self.orn = orn
        self.euler = euler


class dofbot:
    def __init__(self, urdfPath):
        # # upper limits for null space
        self.ll = [-np.pi, 0, 0, 0, -np.pi]
        # upper limits for null space
        self.ul = [np.pi, np.pi, np.pi, np.pi, np.pi]

        # joint ranges for null space
        self.jr = [np.pi * 2.0, np.pi, np.pi, np.pi, 2.0 * np.pi]
        # rest poses for null space
        self.rp = [np.pi / 2.0, np.pi / 2.0, np.pi / 2.0, np.pi / 2.0, np.pi / 2.0]

        self.maxForce = 200.
        self.fingerAForce = 2.5
        self.fingerBForce = 2.5
        self.fingerTipForce = 2

        self.dofbotUid = p.loadURDF(urdfPath,baseOrientation =p.getQuaternionFromEuler([0, 0, 0]), useFixedBase=True)
        # self.numJoints = p.getNumJoints(self.dofbotUid)
        self.numJoints = 5
        self.gripper_joints = [5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 10]

        # self.jointStartPositions = [1.57, 0, 1.57, 1.57, 1.57]
        self.jointStartPositions = [1.57, 1, 1.57, 1.57, 1.57]
        self.desire_qpos = np.array(self.jointStartPositions)
        self.gripperAngle = 0.0

        self.motorIndices = []
        for jointIndex in range(self.numJoints):
            p.resetJointState(self.dofbotUid, jointIndex, self.jointStartPositions[jointIndex])
            qIndex = p.getJointInfo(self.dofbotUid, jointIndex)[3]
            if qIndex > -1:
                self.motorIndices.append(jointIndex)

        self.jointPositions = self.get_jointPoses()

        self.gripperStartAngle = 0.0
        for i, jointIndex in enumerate(self.gripper_joints):
            p.resetJointState(self.dofbotUid, jointIndex, self.gripperStartAngle)


        self.endEffectorPos = []
        self.endEffectorOrn = []
        self.endEffectorEuler = []
        self.endEffectorPos, self.endEffectorOrn, self.endEffectorEuler = self.get_pose()

    def reset(self):
        self.gripperAngle = 0.0
        for jointIndex in range(self.numJoints):
            p.resetJointState(self.dofbotUid, jointIndex, self.jointStartPositions[jointIndex])
        for i, jointIndex in enumerate(self.gripper_joints):
            p.resetJointState(self.dofbotUid, jointIndex, self.gripperAngle)
        self.jointPositions = self.get_jointPoses()
        self.endEffectorPos, self.endEffectorOrn, self.endEffectorEuler = self.get_pose()
        self.desire_qpos = np.array(self.jointStartPositions)

    # def forwardKinematic(self,jointPoses):
    #     for i in range(self.numJoints):
    #         p.resetJointState(self.dofbotUid,
    #                           jointIndex=i,targetValue=jointPoses[i],targetVelocity=0)
    #     return self.get_pose()


    def joint_control(self,dqpos):
        self.desire_qpos = self.desire_qpos + dqpos
        jointPoses = self.desire_qpos
        for i in range(self.numJoints):
            p.setJointMotorControl2(bodyUniqueId=self.dofbotUid, jointIndex=i, controlMode=p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                    targetPosition=jointPoses[i], targetVelocity=0, force=200,
                                    maxVelocity=10.0, positionGain=0.3, velocityGain=1)
        self.jointPositions, self.gripperAngle = self.get_jointPoses()
        self.endEffectorPos, self.endEffectorOrn, self.endEffectorEuler = self.get_pose()
        return self.endEffectorPos, self.endEffectorOrn, self.endEffectorEuler

    def setInverseKine(self, pos, orn):
        if orn == None:
            jointPoses = p.calculateInverseKinematics(self.dofbotUid, 4, pos,
                                                      self.ll, self.ul, self.jr, self.rp)
        else:
            jointPoses = p.calculateInverseKinematics(self.dofbotUid, 4, pos, orn,
                                                      self.ll, self.ul, self.jr, self.rp)
        return jointPoses[:self.numJoints], self.gripperAngle

    def get_jointPoses(self):
        jointPoses= []
        for i in range(self.numJoints+1):
            state = p.getJointState(self.dofbotUid, i)
            jointPoses.append(state[0])
        return jointPoses[:self.numJoints], self.gripperAngle
    
    def get_qvel(self):
        jointVels= []
        for i in range(self.numJoints+1):
            state = p.getJointState(self.dofbotUid, i)
            jointVels.append(state[1])
        return np.array(jointVels[:self.numJoints])

    def update_arrow_display(self, pos, orn):
        arrow_start = pos

        # 长度可自由调节
        arrow_length = 0.3
        # 分别旋转单位向量 [1,0,0], [0,1,0], [0,0,1]（分别对应 X, Y, Z）
        x_dir = p.multiplyTransforms([0, 0, 0], orn, [arrow_length, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0, 1])[0]
        y_dir = p.multiplyTransforms([0, 0, 0], orn, [0, arrow_length, 0], [0, 0, 0, 1])[0]
        z_dir = p.multiplyTransforms([0, 0, 0], orn, [0, 0, arrow_length], [0, 0, 0, 1])[0]

        arrow_end_x = [arrow_start[i] + x_dir[i] for i in range(3)]
        arrow_end_y = [arrow_start[i] + y_dir[i] for i in range(3)]
        arrow_end_z = [arrow_start[i] + z_dir[i] for i in range(3)]

        arrow_items = []
        arrow_items.append(p.addUserDebugLine(
            arrow_start, arrow_end_x, [1, 0, 0], lineWidth=3, lifeTime=0
        ))
        arrow_items.append(p.addUserDebugLine(
            arrow_start, arrow_end_y, [0, 1, 0], lineWidth=3, lifeTime=0
        ))
        arrow_items.append(p.addUserDebugLine(
            arrow_start, arrow_end_z, [0, 0, 1], lineWidth=3, lifeTime=0
        ))

        return arrow_items
    
    def get_pose(self):
        # 1. 收集 6 个 link 的位姿
        indices = [6, 8]
        positions = []
        quaternions = []

        for idx in indices:
            link_state = p.getLinkState(self.dofbotUid, idx)
            positions.append(np.array(link_state[0]))
            quaternions.append(np.array(link_state[1]))

        # 2. 平均位置
        avg_pos = np.mean(positions, axis=0)

        # 3. 平均朝向（四元数）
        rotations = R.from_quat(quaternions)  # scipy 自动归一化
        avg_rot = rotations.mean()
        avg_orn = avg_rot.as_quat()  # [x,y,z,w] 格式
        
        # 4. gripper pos
        grip_pos = R.from_quat(avg_orn).apply(np.array([0, 0, 0.02])) + avg_pos

        # 现在 avg_pos 和 avg_orn 就是“夹爪”整体的均值位姿
        pos = grip_pos
        orn = avg_orn
        euler = p.getEulerFromQuaternion(orn)
        return pos, orn, euler

    def getObservation(self):
        dofbot_obs = dict()
        qpos, gripper = self.get_jointPoses()
        qpos.append(gripper)
        dofbot_obs["qpos"] = np.array(qpos)
        pos, orn, euler = self.get_pose()
        dofbot_obs["eepose"] =np.array(list(pos) + list(orn))
        # self.update_arrow_display(pos, orn)
        
        return dofbot_obs

    def gripper_control(self, gripperAngle):

        p.setJointMotorControl2(self.dofbotUid,
                                5,
                                p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                targetPosition=gripperAngle,
                                force=self.fingerAForce)
        p.setJointMotorControl2(self.dofbotUid,
                                6,
                                p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                targetPosition=gripperAngle,
                                force=self.fingerBForce)
        p.setJointMotorControl2(self.dofbotUid,
                                7,
                                p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                targetPosition=gripperAngle,
                                force=self.fingerAForce)
        p.setJointMotorControl2(self.dofbotUid,
                                8,
                                p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                targetPosition=gripperAngle,
                                force=self.fingerBForce)
        p.setJointMotorControl2(self.dofbotUid,
                                9,
                                p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                targetPosition=gripperAngle,
                                force=self.fingerAForce)
        p.setJointMotorControl2(self.dofbotUid,
                                10,
                                p.POSITION_CONTROL,
                                targetPosition=gripperAngle,
                                force=self.fingerAForce)

        self.gripperAngle = gripperAngle


class Object:
    def __init__(self, urdfPath, block,num):
        self.id = p.loadURDF(urdfPath)
        self.half_height = 0.015 if block else 0.0745
        self.num = num

        self.block = block
    def reset(self):

        if self.num==1:
            # p.resetBasePositionAndOrientation(self.id,
            #                              np.array([ 0.20, 0.1,
            #                                        self.half_height]),
            #                             p.getQuaternionFromEuler([0, 0,np.pi/6]))
            p.resetBasePositionAndOrientation(self.id,
                                         np.array([ 0.18, 0.07,
                                                   self.half_height]),
                                        p.getQuaternionFromEuler([0, 0,np.pi/6]))
        else:
            p.resetBasePositionAndOrientation(self.id,
                                         np.array([ 0.2, -0.1,
                                                   0.005]),
                                        p.getQuaternionFromEuler([0, 0,0]))

    def getObservation(self):
        pos, orn = p.getBasePositionAndOrientation(self.id)
        euler = p.getEulerFromQuaternion(orn)
        return Observation(pos, orn, euler)

    def pos_and_orn(self):
        pos, orn = p.getBasePositionAndOrientation(self.id)
        euler = p.getEulerFromQuaternion(orn)
        return pos, orn, euler


def check_pairwise_collisions(bodies):
    for body1 in bodies:
        for body2 in bodies:
            if body1 != body2 and \
                    len(p.getClosestPoints(bodyA=body1, bodyB=body2, distance=0., physicsClientId=0)) != 0:
                return True
    return False

register(
    id="DofbotReachEnv-v1",
    entry_point="dofbotGymReachEnv:DofbotEnv",
    max_episode_steps=500,
)
class DofbotEnv(gym.Env):
    metadata = {'render_modes': ['human', 'rgb_array']}
    def __init__(self, render_mode="human", physicsClientId=None):
        self._timeStep = 1 / 120
        self.simuRepeatNum = 5
        self.render_mode = render_mode
        # 如果外部已经连好，直接用；否则默认老行为（兼容旧代码）
        if physicsClientId is None:
            if render_mode == "human":
                self.physicsClient = p.connect(p.GUI)
            else:
                self.physicsClient = p.connect(p.DIRECT)
        else:
            self.physicsClient = physicsClientId
        p.resetDebugVisualizerCamera(1.0, 100, -20, [0, 0, 0])
        p.setPhysicsEngineParameter(numSolverIterations=150)
        p.setTimeStep(self._timeStep)
        p.setGravity(0, 0, -9.81)


        p.loadURDF("models/floor.urdf", [0, 0, -0.625], useFixedBase=True)
        p.loadURDF("models/table_collision/table.urdf", [0.5, 0, -0.625],p.getQuaternionFromEuler([0, 0, 0]),
                   useFixedBase=True)
        self._dofbot = dofbot("models/dofbot_urdf_with_gripper/dofbot_with_gripper.urdf")
        self._object1 = Object("models/box_green.urdf", block=True,num=1)
        # self._object2 = Object("models/box_red.urdf", block=True,num=2)
        self.end_effector_arrow_id = None
        self.object_arrow_id = None

        self.target_pos = np.array([0.2, -0.15, 0.15])
        # # 创建红色目标球（无碰撞，仅视觉）
        # target_vis = p.createVisualShape(
        #     shapeType=p.GEOM_SPHERE,
        #     radius=0.005,  # 0.5 cm 小球，可按需调大
        #     rgbaColor=[1, 0, 0, 0.9]  # 红色
        # )
        # # 如果想彻底去掉碰撞，可以把碰撞形状设成一个很小的远点
        # target_col = p.createCollisionShape(p.GEOM_SPHERE, radius=0.001)  # 几乎不占地
        # self.target_body_id = p.createMultiBody(
        #     baseMass=0,  # 固定不动
        #     baseCollisionShapeIndex=target_col,
        #     baseVisualShapeIndex=target_vis,
        #     basePosition=self.target_pos  # 放在目标位置
        # )

        self.end_effector_pos = np.array(self._dofbot.endEffectorPos)
        # # 创建红色目标球（无碰撞，仅视觉）
        # end_vis = p.createVisualShape(
        #     shapeType=p.GEOM_SPHERE,
        #     radius=0.005,  # 5 mm 小球，可按需调大
        #     rgbaColor=[0, 0, 1, 0.9]  # 蓝色
        # )
        # # 如果想彻底去掉碰撞，可以把碰撞形状设成一个很小的远点
        # end_col = p.createCollisionShape(p.GEOM_SPHERE, radius=0.001)  # 几乎不占地
        # self.end_body_id = p.createMultiBody(
        #     baseMass=0,  # 固定不动
        #     baseCollisionShapeIndex=end_col,
        #     baseVisualShapeIndex=end_vis,
        #     basePosition=self.end_effector_pos  # 放在目标位置
        # )

        # TODO: observation space and action space
        # self.observation_space =
        # self.action_space =

    def reset(self, seed=None, options=None):
        super().reset(seed=seed)
        self._object1.reset()
        self._dofbot.reset()
        p.stepSimulation()
        obs = self._get_obs()
        info = self._get_info()
        return obs, info
    
    def is_grasped(self):
        min_force = 0.5
        contact_finger1 = p.getContactPoints(bodyA=self._dofbot.dofbotUid, bodyB=self._object1.id, linkIndexA=6)
        contact_finger2 = p.getContactPoints(bodyA=self._dofbot.dofbotUid, bodyB=self._object1.id, linkIndexA=8)
        if bool(contact_finger1):
            # print("contact_finger1", contact_finger1)
            # print("contact_finger1[7]", contact_finger1[0][7])
            normal1 = abs(contact_finger1[0][7][1])  ## y轴方向力
        else:
            normal1 = 0
        if bool(contact_finger2):
            normal2 = abs(contact_finger2[0][7][1])  ## y轴方向力
        else:
            normal2 = 0
        
        if (normal1 > min_force) and (normal2 > min_force):
            return True
        return False

    # TODO: 增加你觉得必要的info，计算奖励的时候可以调用，获取仿真环境中一些特权信息
    def _get_info(self):
        info = dict()

        return info
    
    def angle_diff(self, q1, q2):
        dot_product = np.dot(q1, q2)
        dot_product = np.clip(dot_product, -1.0, 1.0)
        angle_difference = 2 * np.arccos(dot_product)
        return angle_difference

    # TODO: 完善奖励函数
    def _get_reward(self):
        obs = self._get_obs_dict()
        info = self._get_info()
        
        reward = 0
        return reward
    
    def rotate2grasp_pose(self, pose):
        if pose.shape != (7,):
            raise ValueError("Input pose must be a 7D numpy array.") 
        
        position = pose[:3]  
        quaternion = pose[3:] 
        rotation = R.from_quat(quaternion)
        rotation_x_180 = R.from_euler('x', 180, degrees=True)
        new_rotation = rotation * rotation_x_180
        new_quaternion = new_rotation.as_quat()
        new_pose = np.concatenate([position, new_quaternion])
        return new_pose
    
    def update_arrow_display(self, pos, orn):
        arrow_start = pos

        # 长度可自由调节
        arrow_length = 0.05

        # 分别旋转单位向量 [1,0,0], [0,1,0], [0,0,1]（分别对应 X, Y, Z）
        x_dir = p.multiplyTransforms([0, 0, 0], orn, [arrow_length, 0, 0], [0, 0, 0, 1])[0]
        y_dir = p.multiplyTransforms([0, 0, 0], orn, [0, arrow_length, 0], [0, 0, 0, 1])[0]
        z_dir = p.multiplyTransforms([0, 0, 0], orn, [0, 0, arrow_length], [0, 0, 0, 1])[0]

        arrow_end_x = [arrow_start[i] + x_dir[i] for i in range(3)]
        arrow_end_y = [arrow_start[i] + y_dir[i] for i in range(3)]
        arrow_end_z = [arrow_start[i] + z_dir[i] for i in range(3)]

        arrow_items = []
        arrow_items.append(p.addUserDebugLine(
            arrow_start, arrow_end_x, [1, 0, 0], lineWidth=3, lifeTime=0
        ))
        arrow_items.append(p.addUserDebugLine(
            arrow_start, arrow_end_y, [0, 1, 0], lineWidth=3, lifeTime=0
        ))
        arrow_items.append(p.addUserDebugLine(
            arrow_start, arrow_end_z, [0, 0, 1], lineWidth=3, lifeTime=0
        ))

        return arrow_items
    
    def _get_obs(self):
        Observation = self._get_obs_dict()

        values = list(Observation.values())
        self._observation = np.concatenate([v if isinstance(v, np.ndarray) else np.array([v], dtype=np.int32) for v in values])
        self._observation = self._observation.astype(np.float32)
        if self.end_effector_arrow_id is not None:
            for item in self.end_effector_arrow_id:
                p.removeUserDebugItem(item)

        if self.object_arrow_id is not None:
            for item in self.object_arrow_id:
                p.removeUserDebugItem(item)

        self.end_effector_arrow_id = self.update_arrow_display(Observation["eepose"][:3], Observation["eepose"][3:])
        self.object_arrow_id = self.update_arrow_display(Observation["grasp_pose"][:3], Observation["grasp_pose"][3:])
        return self._observation


    def _get_obs_dict(self):
        Observation = self._dofbot.getObservation()

        # TODO:完善observation

        return Observation

    def step(self, action):
        """
        action - np.array(5)
        """

        # TODO: 完善control指令

        for i in range(self.simuRepeatNum):
            p.stepSimulation()
        
        if self.render_mode == "human":
            time.sleep(self._timeStep)
        terminated = self._termination()
        truncated = False
        self._observation = self._get_obs()
        reward = self._get_reward()
        info = self._get_info()
        return self._observation, reward, terminated, truncated, info

    def _termination(self):
        info = self._get_info()
        if info["success"]:
            return True
        return False
    
    def dofbot_control(self,jointPoses,gripperAngle):
        '''
        :param jointPoses: 数组，机械臂五个关节角度
        :param gripperAngle: 浮点数，机械臂夹爪角度，负值加紧，真值张开
        :return:
        '''
        self._dofbot.joint_control(jointPoses)
        self._dofbot.gripper_control(gripperAngle)
        p.stepSimulation()
        # time.sleep(self._timeStep)

    def dofbot_setInverseKine(self,pos,orn = None):
        '''

        :param pos: 机械臂末端位置，xyz
        :param orn: 机械臂末端方向，四元数
        :return: 机械臂各关节角度
        '''
        jointPoses = self._dofbot.setInverseKine(pos, orn)
        return jointPoses

    # def dofbot_forwardKine(self,jointStates):
    #     return self._dofbot.forwardKinematic(jointStates)

    def get_dofbot_jointPoses(self):
        '''
        :return: 机械臂五个关节位置+夹爪角度
        '''
        jointPoses, gripper_angle = self._dofbot.get_jointPoses()

        return jointPoses, gripper_angle

    def get_dofbot_pose(self):
        '''
        :return: 机械臂末端位姿，xyz+四元数+欧拉角
        '''
        pos, orn, euler = self._dofbot.get_pose()
        return pos, orn, euler

    def get_block_pose(self):
        '''
        :return: 物块位姿，xyz+四元数
        '''
        pos, orn, euler = self._object1.pos_and_orn()
        return pos, orn, euler

    def get_target_pose(self):
        '''
        :return: 目标位置，xyz
        '''
        return self.target_pos

    def set_target_pos(self, target_pos):
        self.target_pos = target_pos
        # p.resetBasePositionAndOrientation(self.target_body_id, target_pos, [0, 0, 0, 1])

### DeepSeek AI

<p>思考：</p><blockquote><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们有两个版本的代码，第一个是dofbotGymReachEnv2.py，第二个是当前提供的代码。第一个版本是一个完整的实现，我们可以参考它来补全当前代码中的TODO部分。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>当前代码的TODO部分包括：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在__init__中：定义observation_space和action_space</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_info中：增加必要的info，用于计算奖励和获取特权信息</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_reward中：完善奖励函数</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_obs_dict中：完善observation</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在step函数中：完善control指令</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>另外，我们注意到第一个版本中有一个DofbotEnv类，它已经实现了一个抓取环境。我们可以参考它的观察空间、动作空间、奖励函数等。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>观察一下当前代码的结构：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>当前代码的DofbotEnv类中，已经有一些初始化，包括加载环境、创建机械臂和物体。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>动作空间：第一个版本中动作空间是6维，包括5个关节和1个夹爪。当前代码中，我们注意到_dofbot有5个关节，夹爪是单独控制的。所以动作空间应该是6维：5个关节动作和1个夹爪动作。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>观察空间：第一个版本中观察空间是23维，包括qpos(6维:5个关节+1个夹爪)、eepose(7维:3位置+4四元数)、grasp_pose(7维:3位置+4四元数)、ee_to_grasp_pos(3维)。但是当前代码中，我们注意到_dofbot的getObservation返回的是qpos(6维)和eepose(7维)，共13维。我们还需要加入grasp_pose和ee_to_grasp_pos。所以观察空间应该是13+7+3=23维。</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们按照第一个版本的思路来补全：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>动作空间：Box(low=-1, high=1, shape=(6,))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>观察空间：Box(low=-inf, high=inf, shape=(23,))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_obs_dict中，我们需要计算grasp_pose和ee_to_grasp_pos。grasp_pose是抓取目标物体的位姿（第一个版本中是在物体上方5cm处，且旋转了180度）。ee_to_grasp_pos是夹爪位置到抓取位置的向量。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_info中，我们需要计算一些信息，比如夹爪与抓取位置的距离、夹爪与抓取姿态的差异、是否抓取、是否成功等。这些信息可以用于奖励函数和终止判断。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_reward中，我们参考第一个版本的奖励函数，根据位置误差、姿态误差、是否抓取、是否成功等给出奖励。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在step函数中，我们需要将动作应用到机械臂和夹爪上。第一个版本中，动作前5个是关节的相对变化，第6个是夹爪动作。当前代码中，我们注意到_dofbot有joint_control和gripper_control方法。我们可以类似地处理：将前5个动作乘以一个系数（如0.05）加到当前关节角度上，然后控制夹爪。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>终止条件：当成功抓取并抬起物体时，终止。</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们按照这个思路来补全代码。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>注意：第一个版本中，夹爪动作是0到1，0表示关闭，1表示打开。而当前代码中，夹爪控制是直接设置一个角度，且我们注意到当前代码中夹爪角度为0时是闭合吗？从reset中夹爪角度为0，且从gripper_control函数看，负值应该是闭合？但是当前代码中gripper_control函数是设置所有夹爪关节为同一个角度，这可能需要调整。但是为了简单，我们暂时按照第一个版本的方式：将动作的第6个分量从[-1,1]映射到[0,1]（因为当前代码的gripper_control函数中，角度为正，且从0开始，我们假设0是闭合，但实际需要测试）。但是第一个版本中，夹爪动作是0（关闭）到1（打开），而当前代码的gripper_control函数中，我们传入的角度是gripperAngle，从reset中初始化为0，且没有说明正负对应开闭。我们参考第一个版本，将夹爪动作映射到[0,1]（0关闭，1打开），然后传入gripper_control。但是当前代码的gripper_control函数中，我们注意到它控制多个关节，且没有区分正负，所以我们需要调整夹爪控制。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>由于当前代码的夹爪控制是设置同一个角度，而实际上我们的夹爪需要对称运动，所以我们可以修改gripper_control，使其接受一个在[0,1]之间的值，0表示闭合，1表示张开。然后内部将其映射到合适的角度。但是为了快速实现，我们暂时按照第一个版本的方式：将动作的第6个分量从[-1,1]映射到[0,1]，然后传入gripper_control。注意，当前代码的gripper_control函数中，我们传入的角度是gripperAngle，在reset中为0，且我们观察夹爪关节，发现它们是对称的。所以我们可以这样映射：当action[5]为1时，夹爪张开（角度为0.03？），当action[5]为-1时，夹爪闭合（角度为0）。但是当前代码的gripper_control函数中，我们传入的角度就是直接设置关节角度，所以我们需要确定一个张开和闭合的角度。从reset中，我们看到夹爪关节初始化为0，且从urdf文件我们无法得知，所以我们假设0是闭合，0.03是张开（类似于第一个版本）。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们定义：</span><br><span>gripper_action = (action[5] + 1) / 2 * 0.03   # 将[-1,1]映射到[0,0.03]</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是注意，第一个版本中，夹爪动作是0（关闭）到1（打开），而当前代码中，我们假设gripper_control传入的角度越大，夹爪张开越大。所以我们这样映射。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>然而，为了与第一个版本保持一致，我们也可以将夹爪动作映射到[0,1]（0关闭，1打开），然后乘以一个最大角度（比如0.03）。所以：</span><br><span>gripper_action = (action[5] + 1) / 2   # 得到[0,1]</span><br><span>然后传入gripper_control时，使用gripper_action * 0.03</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是当前代码的gripper_control函数中，我们传入的角度就是直接设置关节角度，所以我们可以这样。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>现在，我们开始补全代码。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>注意：我们尽量不修改当前代码的非TODO部分，但为了完成功能，我们可能需要在一些地方添加必要的代码。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>步骤：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在__init__中定义观察空间和动作空间。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_info中，计算以下信息：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>dist_pos: 夹爪位置与抓取位置（grasp_pose的位置）的欧氏距离</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>dist_orn: 夹爪姿态与抓取姿态的四元数夹角（用第一个版本的方法）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>is_gripping: 夹爪是否闭合（根据夹爪角度判断，如果夹爪角度小于一个阈值，认为闭合）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>is_grasped: 是否抓取到物体（通过接触判断，我们已经有is_grasped方法，但第一个版本中是用接触点数量，这里我们用了力传感器，所以我们可以用现有的is_grasped方法）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>is_lifted: 物体是否被抬起（物体位置高度大于某个值）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>success: 是否成功（is_lifted and is_grasped）</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_reward中，根据上述信息计算奖励。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在_get_obs_dict中，计算grasp_pose和ee_to_grasp_pos。grasp_pose的计算方法参考第一个版本：在物体位置上方5cm，且旋转180度（绕x轴旋转180度）。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在step函数中，将动作分解为关节动作和夹爪动作，并应用到机械臂上。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>修改终止条件：当成功时终止。</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>由于代码较长，我们只补全TODO部分，并确保代码能运行。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们开始写代码。</span></p></blockquote><br/><p <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Observation</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> pos<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> euler<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pos <span class="token operator">=</span> pos

<span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">dofbot</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">__init__</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> urdfPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># # upper limits for null space</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ll <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token operator">-</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">-</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        <span class="token comment"># upper limits for null space</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ul <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">]</span>

        <span class="token comment"># joint ranges for null space</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>jr <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi<span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        <span class="token comment"># rest poses for null space</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rp <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pi <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>maxForce <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">200.</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>fingerAForce <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">2.5</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>fingerBForce <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">2.5</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>fingerTipForce <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">2</span>

        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dofbotUid <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>loadURDF<span class="token punctuation">(</span>urdfPath<span class="token punctuation">,</span>baseOrientation <span class="token operator">=</span>p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getQuaternionFromEuler<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> useFixedBase<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token comment"># self.numJoints = p.getNumJoints(self.dofbotUid)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>numJoints <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">5</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gripper_joints <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">7</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">9</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">get_pose</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 1. 收集 6 个 link 的位姿</span>
        indices <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        positions <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        quaternions <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

        <span class="token keyword">for</span> idx <span class="token keyword">in</span> indices<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            link_state <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getLinkState<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dofbotUid<span class="token punctuation">,</span> idx<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            positions<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span>link_state<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            quaternions<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span>link_state<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

        <span class="token comment"># 2. 平均位置</span>
        avg_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>positions<span class="token punctuation">,</span> axis<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

        <span class="token comment"># 3. 平均朝向（四元数）</span>
        rotations <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>quaternions<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># scipy 自动归一化</span>
        avg_rot <span class="token operator">=</span> rotations<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        avg_orn <span class="token operator">=</span> avg_rot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>as_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># [x,y,z,w] 格式</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 4. gripper pos</span>
        grip_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>avg_orn<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">apply</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0.02</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> avg_pos

        <span class="token comment"># 现在 avg_pos 和 avg_orn 就是"夹爪"整体的均值位姿</span>
        pos <span class="token operator">=</span> grip_pos
        orn <span class="token operator">=</span> avg_orn
        euler <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getEulerFromQuaternion<span class="token punctuation">(</span>orn<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn<span class="token punctuation">,</span> euler

        <span class="token comment"># )</span>

        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>end_effector_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>endEffectorPos<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token comment"># # 创建红色目标球（无碰撞，仅视觉）</span>
        <span class="token comment"># end_vis = p.createVisualShape(</span>
        <span class="token comment">#     shapeType=p.GEOM_SPHERE,</span>

        <span class="token comment">#     rgbaColor=[0, 0, 1, 0.9]  # 蓝色</span>
        <span class="token comment"># )</span>
        <span class="token comment"># # 如果想彻底去掉碰撞，可以把碰撞形状设成一个很小的远点</span>
        <span class="token comment"># end_col = p.createCollisionShape(p.GEOM_SPHERE, radius=0.001)  # 几乎不占地</span>
        <span class="token comment"># self.end_body_id = p.createMultiBody(</span>

        <span class="token comment">#     basePosition=self.end_effector_pos  # 放在目标位置</span>

        <span class="token comment"># TODO: observation space and action space</span>
        <span class="token comment"># self.observation_space =</span>
        <span class="token comment"># self.action_space =</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 补全观察空间和动作空间</span>
        obs_dim <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">23</span>  <span class="token comment"># 参考第一个文件中的观察维度</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>observation_space <span class="token operator">=</span> spaces<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Box<span class="token punctuation">(</span>low<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token operator">-</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>inf<span class="token punctuation">,</span> high<span class="token operator">=</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>inf<span class="token punctuation">,</span> shape<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>obs_dim<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> dtype<span class="token operator">=</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>float32<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>action_space <span class="token operator">=</span> spaces<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Box<span class="token punctuation">(</span>low<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> high<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> shape<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> dtype<span class="token operator">=</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>float32<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> seed<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> options<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">None</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token builtin">super</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>reset<span class="token punctuation">(</span>seed<span class="token operator">=</span>seed<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">is_grasped</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        min_force <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0.5</span>
        contact_finger1 <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getContactPoints<span class="token punctuation">(</span>bodyA<span class="token operator">=</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dofbotUid<span class="token punctuation">,</span> bodyB<span class="token operator">=</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_object1<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> linkIndexA<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        contact_finger2 <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getContactPoints<span class="token punctuation">(</span>bodyA<span class="token operator">=</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dofbotUid<span class="token punctuation">,</span> bodyB<span class="token operator">=</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_object1<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">id</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> linkIndexA<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token builtin">bool</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>contact_finger1<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token comment"># print("contact_finger1", contact_finger1)</span>
            <span class="token comment"># print("contact_finger1[7]", contact_finger1[0][7])</span>
            normal1 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token builtin">abs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>contact_finger1<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">7</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">## y轴方向力</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            normal1 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token builtin">bool</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>contact_finger2<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            normal2 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token builtin">abs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>contact_finger2<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">7</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment">## y轴方向力</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            normal2 <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>normal1 <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> min_force<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>normal2 <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> min_force<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token boolean">True</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token boolean">False</span>

    <span class="token comment"># TODO: 增加你觉得必要的info，计算奖励的时候可以调用，获取仿真环境中一些特权信息</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">_get_info</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        info <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token builtin">dict</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 获取机械臂和物体信息</span>
        ee_pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> ee_orn<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _ <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_pose<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        obj_pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _ <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_object1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pos_and_orn<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算抓取位姿</span>
        grasp_pose <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_calculate_grasp_pose<span class="token punctuation">(</span>obj_pos<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        grasp_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> grasp_pose<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算位置和姿态距离</span>
        info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"dist_pos"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>linalg<span class="token punctuation">.</span>norm<span class="token punctuation">(</span>ee_pos <span class="token operator">-</span> grasp_pos<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 计算姿态差异</span>
        ee_quat <span class="token operator">=</span> ee_orn
        grasp_quat <span class="token operator">=</span> grasp_pose<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        dot_product <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">abs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dot<span class="token punctuation">(</span>ee_quat<span class="token punctuation">,</span> grasp_quat<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"dist_orn"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">2</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>arccos<span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dot_product<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 获取夹爪状态</span>
        _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> gripper_angle <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_jointPoses<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"is_gripping"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token builtin">abs</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>gripper_angle<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">&lt;</span> <span class="token number">0.01</span>  <span class="token comment"># 夹爪角度小于0.01认为在抓取</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 检查是否成功抓取和抬起</span>
        is_grasped <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>is_grasped<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        is_lifted <span class="token operator">=</span> obj_pos<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_object1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>half_height <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">0.03</span>
        info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"is_lifted"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> is_lifted <span class="token keyword">and</span> is_grasped
        info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"success"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"is_lifted"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> info
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">angle_diff</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> q1<span class="token punctuation">,</span> q2<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        dot_product <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dot<span class="token punctuation">(</span>q1<span class="token punctuation">,</span> q2<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        dot_product <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dot_product<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        angle_difference <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">2</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>arccos<span class="token punctuation">(</span>dot_product<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> angle_difference

    <span class="token comment"># TODO: 完善奖励函数</span>
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">_get_reward</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        info <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_get_info<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 基础奖励基于位置和姿态距离</span>
        reward <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1.0</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"dist_pos"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">-</span> <span class="token number">0.5</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"dist_orn"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 如果靠近抓取位置且姿态正确，给予额外奖励</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"dist_pos"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">&lt;</span> <span class="token number">0.03</span> <span class="token keyword">and</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"dist_orn"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">&lt;</span> <span class="token number">0.5</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            reward <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span>
            
            <span class="token comment"># 如果夹爪在抓取位置，给予额外奖励</span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"is_gripping"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                reward <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">1.0</span>
                
                <span class="token comment"># 如果成功抓取物体，给予额外奖励</span>
                <span class="token keyword">if</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>is_grasped<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
                    reward <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">2.0</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 如果成功完成任务，给予大量奖励</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> info<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">"success"</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            reward <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">20.0</span>
            
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> reward
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">rotate2grasp_pose</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> pose<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> pose<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shape <span class="token operator">!=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">7</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            <span class="token keyword">raise</span> ValueError<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"Input pose must be a 7D numpy array."</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> 
        
        position <span class="token operator">=</span> pose<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>  
        quaternion <span class="token operator">=</span> pose<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> 
        rotation <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>quaternion<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        rotation_x_180 <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_euler<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'x'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">180</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> degrees<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        new_rotation <span class="token operator">=</span> rotation <span class="token operator">*</span> rotation_x_180
        new_quaternion <span class="token operator">=</span> new_rotation<span class="token punctuation">.</span>as_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        new_pose <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>concatenate<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>position<span class="token punctuation">,</span> new_quaternion<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> new_pose
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">update_arrow_display</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        arrow_start <span class="token operator">=</span> pos

        <span class="token comment"># 长度可自由调节</span>
        arrow_length <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0.05</span>

        <span class="token comment"># 分别旋转单位向量 [1,0,0], [0,1,0], [0,0,1]（分别对应 X, Y, Z）</span>
        x_dir <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>multiplyTransforms<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>arrow_length<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        y_dir <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>multiplyTransforms<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> arrow_length<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        z_dir <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>multiplyTransforms<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> arrow_length<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

        <span class="token comment"># TODO:完善observation</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 添加抓取位姿和末端到抓取位置的向量</span>
        obj_pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _ <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_object1<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pos_and_orn<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">_calculate_grasp_pose</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> obj_pos<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 计算抓取位姿 - 在物体上方5cm处，旋转180度</span>
        grasp_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> obj_pos<span class="token punctuation">.</span>copy<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        grasp_pos<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">0.05</span>
        grasp_orn <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_euler<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'xyz'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">180</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> degrees<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token boolean">True</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>as_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>concatenate<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>grasp_pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> grasp_orn<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">step</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token triple-quoted-string string">"""
        action - np.array(6)
        """</span>

        <span class="token comment"># TODO: 完善control指令</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 将动作分解为关节控制和夹爪控制</span>
        action <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>clip<span class="token punctuation">(</span>action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>action_space<span class="token punctuation">.</span>low<span class="token punctuation">,</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>action_space<span class="token punctuation">.</span>high<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        joint_action<span class="token punctuation">,</span> gripper_action <span class="token operator">=</span> action<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> action<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">5</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 应用关节控制</span>
        current_joint_poses<span class="token punctuation">,</span> _ <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>get_jointPoses<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        target_joint_poses <span class="token operator">=</span> current_joint_poses <span class="token operator">+</span> joint_action <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.05</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>joint_control<span class="token punctuation">(</span>target_joint_poses<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 应用夹爪控制 - 将[-1,1]映射到[0,0.03]</span>
        gripper_angle <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>gripper_action <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.03</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_dofbot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gripper_control<span class="token punctuation">(</span>gripper_angle<span class="token punctuation">)</span>

        <span class="token keyword">for</span> i <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>simuRepeatNum<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>stepSimulation<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>render_mode <span class="token operator">==</span> <span class="token string">"human"</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            time<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sleep<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_timeStep<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        terminated <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_termination<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        truncated <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">False</span>
        self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_observation <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_get_obs<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        reward <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_get_reward<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        info <span class="token operator">=</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_get_info<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>_observation<span class="token punctuation">,</span> reward<span class="token punctuation">,</span> terminated<span class="token punctuation">,</span> truncated<span class="token punctuation">,</span> info

            <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token boolean">True</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token boolean">False</span>
    
    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">dofbot_control</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">,</span>jointPoses<span class="token punctuation">,</span>gripperAngle<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>

### DeepSeek AI

<p>思考：</p><blockquote><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>根据错误信息，问题出现在</span>`_calculate_grasp_pose`<span>方法中，我们尝试对一个元组调用</span>`copy`<span>方法。</span><br><span>在</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>方法中，我们调用了</span>`self._object1.pos_and_orn()`<span>，它返回的是一个元组，我们只取了第一个元素（位置）吗？</span><br><span>实际上，</span>`pos_and_orn`<span>方法返回的是</span>`(pos, orn, euler)`<span>，所以我们应该是要取第一个元素作为位置。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是，在</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>中，我们是这样获取物体位置的：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span><br><span>这里</span>`obj_pos`<span>应该是一个表示位置的元组（或列表），而元组没有</span>`copy`<span>方法。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们可以将元组转换为numpy数组，或者直接使用元组，但是注意在</span>`_calculate_grasp_pose`<span>中我们使用了</span>`copy`<span>方法，所以我们可以先将其转换为numpy数组。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>修改</span>`_calculate_grasp_pose`<span>方法，将传入的</span>`obj_pos`<span>转换为numpy数组，然后再使用</span>`copy`<span>。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是，我们也可以修改</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>中获取物体位置的方式，确保它是numpy数组。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>让我们检查一下</span>`Object`<span>类的</span>`pos_and_orn`<span>方法，它返回的是：</span><br><span>return pos, orn, euler</span><br><span>其中，</span>`pos`<span>是</span>`p.getBasePositionAndOrientation`<span>返回的元组，所以是一个三元组。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们可以将</span>`obj_pos`<span>转换为numpy数组，然后再传递给</span>`_calculate_grasp_pose`<span>。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>修改</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>中的代码：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>将：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span><br><span>grasp_pose = self._calculate_grasp_pose(obj_pos)</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>改为：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span><br><span>obj_pos = np.array(obj_pos)  # 转换为numpy数组</span><br><span>grasp_pose = self._calculate_grasp_pose(obj_pos)</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这样，在</span>`_calculate_grasp_pose`<span>中，</span>`obj_pos`<span>就是numpy数组，具有</span>`copy`<span>方法。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>另外，我们还需要注意，在</span>`_get_info`<span>方法中，我们也使用了</span>`obj_pos`<span>，同样需要转换。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是，在</span>`_get_info`<span>中，我们是从</span>`self._object1.pos_and_orn()`<span>获取的位置，也是元组。所以我们也需要修改</span>`_get_info`<span>：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>将：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>改为：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span><br><span>obj_pos = np.array(obj_pos)</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这样，在</span>`_get_info`<span>中计算距离时，</span>`obj_pos`<span>和</span>`ee_pos`<span>（numpy数组）之间的运算就不会有问题。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是，我们也要注意，在</span>`is_grasped`<span>方法中，我们使用了</span>`self._object1.id`<span>，没有使用位置，所以不用改。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>让我们修改这两处。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>另外，在</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>中，我们还要注意，我们使用</span>`Observation`<span>（一个字典）来收集观察值，然后将其转换为一个长的numpy数组。我们添加的</span>`grasp_pose`<span>和</span>`ee_to_grasp_pos`<span>都应该是numpy数组。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们进行如下修改：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在</span>`_get_info`<span>中，将物体位置转换为numpy数组。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>中，将物体位置转换为numpy数组。</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>修改后的代码：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在</span>`_get_info`<span>方法中：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span><br><span>obj_pos = np.array(obj_pos)   # 添加这一行</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>方法中：</span><br><span>obj_pos, _, _ = self._object1.pos_and_orn()</span><br><span>obj_pos = np.array(obj_pos)   # 添加这一行</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这样，应该可以解决元组没有copy方法的问题。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但是，我们也要注意，在</span>`_calculate_grasp_pose`<span>方法中，我们使用了</span>`obj_pos.copy()`<span>，现在</span>`obj_pos`<span>是numpy数组，所以没问题。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们重新运行代码，看看是否修复了这个错误。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果还有其他错误，我们再根据错误信息进行修复。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>由于代码较长，我只修改错误指向的部分，其他部分保持不变。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>注意：由于我们修改了</span>`_get_info`<span>和</span>`_get_obs_dict`<span>，确保在每次获取物体位置后都转换为numpy数组。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>现在，我们重新提供修改后的代码，只修改了这两个方法。</span></p></blockquote><br/><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这个错误是因为在 </span>`_get_obs_dict`<span> 方法中，</span>`self._object1.pos_and_orn()`<span> 返回的是一个元组，而不是单独的 </span>`obj_pos`<span>。我们需要正确地解包这个元组。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>让我修复这个问题：</span></p><div class="md-code-block <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">Observation</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>

    <span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">get_pose</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        <span class="token comment"># 1. 收集 6 个 link 的位姿</span>
        indices <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">8</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        positions <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
        quaternions <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span>

        <span class="token keyword">for</span> idx <span class="token keyword">in</span> indices<span class="token punctuation">:</span>
            link_state <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getLinkState<span class="token punctuation">(</span>self<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dofbotUid<span class="token punctuation">,</span> idx<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            positions<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span>link_state<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            quaternions<span class="token punctuation">.</span>append<span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span>link_state<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

        <span class="token comment"># 2. 平均位置</span>
        avg_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>positions<span class="token punctuation">,</span> axis<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

        <span class="token comment"># 3. 平均朝向（四元数）</span>
        rotations <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>quaternions<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># scipy 自动归一化</span>
        avg_rot <span class="token operator">=</span> rotations<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        avg_orn <span class="token operator">=</span> avg_rot<span class="token punctuation">.</span>as_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># [x,y,z,w] 格式</span>
        
        <span class="token comment"># 4. gripper pos</span>
        grip_pos <span class="token operator">=</span> R<span class="token punctuation">.</span>from_quat<span class="token punctuation">(</span>avg_orn<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token builtin">apply</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>np<span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0.02</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> avg_pos

        <span class="token comment"># 现在 avg_pos 和 avg_orn 就是"夹爪"整体的均值位姿</span>
        pos <span class="token operator">=</span> grip_pos
        orn <span class="token operator">=</span> avg_orn
        euler <span class="token operator">=</span> p<span class="token punctuation">.</span>getEulerFromQuaternion<span class="token punctuation">(</span>orn<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> pos<span class="token punctuation">,</span> orn<span class="token punctuation">,</span> euler
